{"nick":"joepie91","message":"bybb: serious advice for minimizing bugs: 1) always assume that you will screw up, and account for that, 2) always prefer loud (and crashy) failures over quietly doing the wrong thing, 3) modularize constantly, 4) try to solve every problem by removing code before you try to add code, 5) copy-pasting is forbidden - if you think you need to copy-paste, you either need a third-party module or should abstract your own code","date":"2016-10-12T08:52:52.175Z","type":"message"}
